Huge Case of Pirates Robbing Ships and Kidnapping Police in Wusong Paotai Bay

Police Officer Tian Honghe Narrowly Escapes Being Killed by Pirates

Three Captured Pirates Confess to the Whereabouts of Their Gang Leader

At approximately 5:00 PM the night before last, the Wusong Fourth Squad of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team discovered a large wooden ship loaded with timber near the customs area outside Paotai Bay in Wusong. As the officers boarded the wooden ship to investigate, the pirates, who had been alerted in advance, captured one of the officers and confined him in the hold. The remaining officers jumped into the river and swam to safety. Upon hearing the news, the General Team immediately notified all teams by telephone to mobilize with weapons and, together with the chief of the Seventh District General Office, rushed to surround and suppress the pirates. However, the pirates, realizing the situation was dire, had already boarded another ship and fled out to sea. It was not until dawn the next day that a pirate ship was intercepted, and three pirates were captured. The three pirates confessed to the location of a large-scale pirate den, with more than a thousand members. The details are as follows:

Police Officer Kidnapped At approximately 5:00 PM the day before yesterday, a large ship fully loaded with timber suddenly arrived and anchored near the customs area outside Paotai Bay in Wusong. In the evening, shadows could be seen moving on the ship, and voices were heard. This was discovered by Li Wenhan, a patrol officer of the Wusong Fourth Squad of the Water Patrol Team of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, who found it suspicious. Therefore, at approximately 11:00 PM, he dispatched four police officers, Hou Bengui, Tian Honghe, Du Wentang, and Wang Shuchen, on a sampan to approach the wooden ship to investigate the truth. Unexpectedly, more than twenty pirates, each armed with guns, swarmed out of the hold. They first grabbed Police Officer Tian Honghe, tied him up with rope, and pushed him into the hold.

Large Force Sent to Arrest Upon seeing this, Police Officer Hou Bengui, who was behind, realized the situation was dire. He immediately turned around, jumped back onto the sampan, and sped back to the team to report to Patrol Officer Li. The remaining two police officers, Du Wentang and Wang Shuchen, seeing the urgency of the situation, jumped onto the stern of the ship and, disregarding everything else, plunged into the river and swam back to the team. After receiving the report from Police Officer Hou, Patrol Officer Li immediately reported to the South City General Team and the Seventh District General Office, requesting assistance. The General Team Leader, Zhu Haishan, upon receiving this alarm, immediately accompanied Deputy Team Leader Li Chenghua, personally supervising Patrol Officer Pan Xutong, and, together with Seventh District Chief Gong Xikui, Fourth Squad Patrol Officer Li Wenhan, and more than one hundred police sergeants and officers, all fully armed, boarded multiple steamships and rushed to the scene overnight.

Abandoned Weapons and Fled Upon arriving near the Customs area outside Paotai Bay in Wusong, they first surrounded the large wooden ship. Then they rushed onto the ship to arrest the pirates. The pirates, seeing Police Officer Hou Bengui and others flee in different directions, realized they would report to the police and that the officers would come to suppress them. Therefore, they boarded a ship fully loaded with kerosene and sailed directly out of the Wusongkou, fleeing the scene. When General Team Leader Zhu and others boarded the wooden ship, there was no trace of the pirates. All that remained was a ship of timber, the ship's captain Lin Xingzhong, the crew members Miao Santao, Lin Niansan, Feng Abin, and three rifles and fifty-five rounds of ammunition abandoned by the pirates as they fled.

Accomplices Intercepted Lin, the captain, and the others were immediately detained, and a search of the hold revealed the kidnapped Police Officer Tian Honghe still inside. After rescuing him from the hold, the police dispersed to search the riverbanks inside and outside Wusongkou. At approximately 3:00 AM yesterday, the police intercepted a sampan near Bailonggang on the Pudong side, traveling rapidly from east to west. There were three men on board, whose behavior appeared suspicious. They were immediately ordered to stop and the police boarded the boat. After questioning the men, their answers were evasive. They were detained and taken back to the South City Water Patrol General Team.

Police Officer Nearly Killed However, the kerosene ship used by the pirates escaped to sea on the rising tide, and its whereabouts are unknown. Therefore, Team Leaders Zhu and Li and District Chief Gong continued the siege until dawn, but still did not see any trace of the pirate ship. It was already approximately 6:00 AM. The police then returned separately. Subsequently, at approximately 9:00 AM, Team Leaders Zhu and Li separately interrogated the captured criminals. First, Police Officer Tian Honghe stated that after he was kidnapped last night, the pirates wanted to shoot him. At that time, one of the pirates, who appeared to be the leader, said, "As long as he (referring to me) doesn't make a sound, spare his life." After speaking, he ordered another pirate to stuff a piece of cotton in my mouth so that I couldn't speak. Then they boarded a ship and fled, and so on.

Ship Owner's Testimony The ship's captain, Lin Xingzhong, testified that he was 57 years old and from Huangyan, Zhejiang. He said, "My ship is named Jinshuntai. On the 28th day of the tenth lunar month of this year, I loaded a ship of timber from Wenzhou on behalf of a customer and was transporting it to Chongming. Unexpectedly, when sailing through the waters of Bai Ban Yang, dozens of pirates suddenly appeared, each armed with guns. They boarded my ship and forced me to sail to Shanghai. Along the way, they forced us to provide them with food. Yesterday, my ship was forced to sail to the customs area outside Wusongkou. I was about to go ashore to report to the police when two pirates, each holding a pistol, secretly pressed them against my waist and forced me to go to customs to declare the cargo and then sail into Wusongkou and anchor there. Fortunately, the police discovered this and came to suppress the pirates. Otherwise, the pirates would have stolen the entire ship of timber," and so on.

Confession of Pirate Leader The crew members Miao Santao, Lin Niansan, and Feng Abin gave confessions consistent with Lin's testimony. They identified the three men on the intercepted sampan as pirates. The three pirates were then questioned one by one. One pirate, named Li Chenglai, age 37, from Haimen, Taizhou, confessed that "Our mountain stronghold is on Xijishan Mountain in Haimen, Taizhou. The chieftain is Xiang Langao. There are also Tiannanwang Li Kexing, Wang Laowu, Jin Maorong, Li Yongxing, and others as leaders. We have more than a thousand brothers and plenty of weapons. We usually intercept merchant ships in various sea areas. This time, Li Kexing led us, nineteen brothers in total, each armed with guns, to attempt to rob in the waters of Bai Ban Yang.

Sent to the Bureau for Investigation "We then hijacked the wooden ship and forced it to sail to Shanghai, intending to return to the mountain and boast to the chieftain. Unexpectedly, we were discovered by the police, who came to suppress us. Leader Li and others then boarded a ship and fled elsewhere. However, at that time, I happened to be going to Pudong for business, so I didn't notice, which led to our arrest by the police when we were returning to the ship on a sampan. If the government wants to destroy our stronghold, it must go there on warships. We can lead you there to capture them. Otherwise, not only will you not succeed, but our lives will also be difficult to protect," and so on. Another pirate, named Li Laowu, age 19, confessed. And still another pirate, named Li Zhenglai, of the same age as Laowu, confessed. The rest of their statements were the same as Li Chenglai's. Considering the extreme importance of this case, an official document was immediately prepared, and the prisoners were sent to the bureau for interrogation at approximately 4:00 PM that afternoon.

Huang Fenghao Escapes Danger

Rescued at Caijiaqiao, Zhenru

Detective Team Captures Several Kidnappers

Huang Fenghao, a local accountant at the Xinxing Milk Shed at No. 1040 Great West Road in Shanghai, was suddenly kidnapped by bandits at the intersection of Dunxin Road at 5:15 PM on the 26th of this month and disappeared without a trace. Details have been recorded in this newspaper. After the incident, Detective Team Leader Lu Ying and Sixth District Chief Tan paid close attention. They ordered Tang Bingxiang, the head of the Sixth District Detective Team, to investigate. In just two days, the hostage was rescued, and five kidnappers and two pistols were captured. The details of the successful resolution of the case are recorded below:

Joint Investigation Because the incident occurred within the boundaries of the road being built across the border, the head of the Jing'an Temple police station dispatched Chinese Deputy Inspector Fan Defu to investigate the scene on the afternoon before last. At the time, Team Leader Tang also went to the scene. They jointly inquired with Wang Baocheng, the clerk of the Asia Gas Station there. They learned that the car used by the kidnappers was a black-plated number 400, but the last character was not clearly remembered.

Clues to Solving the Case The police station then investigated numbers 4001 to 4010 based on this number. Only the owner of car number 4003, Shen Guanquan, a local resident living at No. 1798 Jing'an Temple Road, who worked as a driver, was suspected. Detectives were dispatched to arrest Shen. A telephone call was made to the Sixth District, and Team Leader Tang personally went to bring Shen back to the district.

Kidnappers Arrested According to Shen Guanquan's confession, the car, number 4003, was rented to a man named Zhu Sanmao through a friend named Shen Jingen. Zhu lived at No. 10 Wangjia Lane, Yidingpan Road, and so on. After obtaining the confession, Team Leader Tang, at midnight the night before last, led detectives Sun Shucheng, Zhou Wenhai, Cao Chuqiao, Zhang Yuzhu, and police sergeant Shen Jinzhang, disguised themselves and secretly went to the address. Zhu Sanmao, Shen Jingen, and Mao Qiushen were successively arrested and brought back to the district. According to the confession of Shen and Zhu, Huang Fenghao was kidnapped and is currently hidden in a straw hut at Caijiaqiao, Zhenru. They could lead the way.

Hostage Rescued After obtaining the confession, Team Leader Tang reported to District Chief Tan and, along with the original detective team, rushed to Caijiaqiao at 4:00 AM yesterday. They first surrounded the house and then bravely rushed in. They rescued the hostage, Huang Fenghao, and arrested the kidnappers guarding him, Wu Jie, Chen Adi, and Zhao Linsheng, on the spot. They also seized two pistols, thirteen rounds of ammunition, and a pair of sunglasses, and brought them all back to the district. Huang's family was then notified to come to the district to retrieve Huang. After separate interrogation by the district officers, it was decided to prepare an official document and send them to the bureau for interrogation. The kidnapped car was also found yesterday morning on Rue Père Robert in the French Concession and was retrieved by the detective team after notification from the French police station.

The Zhu Baoyuan Estate Dispute Continues

The Dispute Centers on Investigating the Accounts

Rescheduled for Further Questioning of Witnesses on January 10

Zhu Baoyuan, a native of Hai'ning and owner of the Zhenhe Tea Firm, passed away in April of this year, leaving an estate of over 2.7 million yuan. His two eldest sons, Zhu Yanqing and Zhu Shunqing, controlled the estate, while his second wife, Zhu Xinxinbao, and his three unmarried daughters were not allowed to share in the estate. They were all resentful and successively filed lawsuits with the First Special District Local Court, requesting a judgment ordering Yanqing and Shunqing to hand over the entire estate for distribution according to shares. Later, the brothers Yanqing enlisted people to mediate, so their two married sisters, having each received 80,000 yuan, withdrew their lawsuits. However, the amount requested by their stepmother, Zhu Xinxinbao, was over 600,000 yuan. Although Fang Jiaobo and others had acted as mediators, the lack of sincerity on the part of Yanqing and others rendered the efforts fruitless. Moreover, the defendants

Repeatedly Failed to Appear in Court Therefore, the matter remains unresolved to this day. Recently, the plaintiff submitted a request to the court for an order requiring the defendant to submit a list of all assets for verification. The Zhu brothers, knowing that they could not simply gloss over the matter, had to comply. However, the plaintiff was extremely dissatisfied with the list. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Qiao Wanxuan held a further hearing. At that time, the plaintiff's lawyer, Chen Ying, pointed out the shortcomings in the list one by one and attacked them, leading to a heated debate with the defendant's lawyer. According to Lawyer Chen, during the previous court hearing, the court had granted permission for the plaintiff to participate in the examination of the accounts. My lawyer then agreed with the other party to go to the Zhenhe Tea Firm at 9:30 AM on the 25th to examine the accounts opened by the defendant,

Item by Item Scrutiny He also submitted five or six account books, such as the temporary guest ledger of Zhenhe Tea Firm, but they were all from last year. The account books from this year were not submitted at all. Only one monthly statement was provided, which was from this year. In the monthly statement, the rent item for January was recorded as over 360,000 taels of silver, while in June, because the currency had been changed from taels to yuan, it was recorded as over 360,000 yuan. If calculated based on silver and yuan, this one item alone is off by over 100,000. Other properties in Shanghai and Hangzhou, and the amount of monthly rent received from them were asked of the defendant, but he was unwilling to disclose them. Over 400,000 yuan of domestic public bonds, currently worth 280,000 yuan, and its location were not stated. The total amount of foreign stocks was over 250,000 yuan. It was said that 20,000 yuan had been mortgaged. Whether it was completely mortgaged or only a portion had been mortgaged was not stated even when asked. In addition, there were various stocks worth over 36,000 yuan, which were also not disclosed,

Location of Assets The defendant's intention at the time was to simply submit a few ordinary account books and pass them off as a perfunctory effort, not a sincere examination of the accounts. Zhu Yanqing had always managed these shared assets, so he was naturally familiar with the details. Now, he repeatedly said that he did not know, which was clearly an excuse. There was also an item in the accounts for a loan of 50,000 taels of silver from the Asia East Bank, which was said to be borrowed from the Renji Company opened by Shi Shaochu. However, according to what the plaintiff knew, the company was actually founded by Baoyuan with his own funds. Therefore, he requested that Shi Shaochu be summoned to court next time to testify. In short, what is in dispute in this case

The amount of the estate The plaintiff had long asserted that it was over 2.7 million yuan. Even based on the list submitted by the defendant, it was over 900,000 yuan. Therefore, there must be many account books, certainly not just the ones submitted by the defendant. Therefore, the plaintiff should now request two things from the court: (1) The defendant should submit all account books from previous years completely, without concealing anything; (2) The plaintiff should be allowed to bring an accountant to the Zhenhe Tea Firm to verify the accounts. The defendant's representative lawyer strongly opposed both of the plaintiff's requests, stating that Baoyuan's estate was not as large as the plaintiff claimed and that there were no handwritten account books of assets. Zhenhe was still in operation, so this year's account books could not be submitted under any circumstances. If the accounts were to be forcibly seized, then Zhenhe would

Inevitably be Forced to Close At that time, Zhenhe's debt of 240,000 yuan would have to be repaid, and the debt of 260,000 yuan would likely be sacrificed. Would the plaintiff be willing to bear this loss? Therefore, the defendant strongly opposed the seizure of the account books. He could not agree to the examination of the accounts with an accountant, because the plaintiff's lawsuit was for the division of the estate, not for the investigation of the accounts. Why should he add extra complications? Therefore, he firmly opposed it. The plaintiff's lawyer then stated that in order to divide the estate, it was necessary to first examine the accounts in order to understand whether the defendant had concealed any assets. Baoyuan did have handwritten account books of assets, which were taken by the defendant after his death when the plaintiff moved out of the house. The plaintiff should testify in court, and so on. The two lawyers debated with each other for a long time. Finally, it was requested that the defendant be summoned to court next time and that additional witnesses be summoned, which Judge Qiao approved. It was already late in the evening. The court ordered that the hearing be rescheduled for January 10.

Measures for the China Child Welfare Association to Rescue Young Prostitutes

Three Rescue Measures Proposed

To be Implemented After Government Approval

The Shanghai China Child Welfare Association will conduct an on-site investigation of young prostitutes starting on January 1 of the 23rd year of the Republic, and will request that the government provide practical and financial assistance so that young prostitutes have the opportunity to be educated. The outline of the measures to rescue young prostitutes is as follows: (1) On-site investigation: The association, together with government officials, will investigate the living conditions of prostitutes in the Public Concession, the British Concession, the French Concession, the border between the Chinese and Foreign concessions, and the wharves of land and water transportation, ascertain the proportion of young prostitutes, report to local authorities, and find ways to take them in; (2) Establishment of a reporting office: The association plans to rent a house near the Great World to serve as the office address. Prostitutes who cannot bear the suffering and suddenly realize their situation can report themselves, or others can report on their behalf. After their grievances have been redressed, they will be sent to a training institute for care; (3) Establishment of a training institute: Prostitutes whose grievances have been redressed by the association can be sent to a training institute. In addition to providing them with appropriate education every day, they will also be taught simple crafts so that prostitutes who suddenly realize their situation can have the opportunity to acquire skills and general knowledge. Those whose addresses have been ascertained will be taken back by their families. Those whose addresses are unknown will be introduced by the association to appropriate jobs. It is understood that these measures will be implemented after being approved by the government authorities.

A Buyout's Fraudulent Scheme of Setting Up a Shipping Company in a Small Room

Issuing Tens of Thousands of Dollars in Bad Checks

Rice Shops and Leather Shops All Defrauded of Large Sums of Money

Recently, a man named Wang Zhihua from Zhenhai, Ningbo, 34 years old, due to extreme boredom, conceived a whimsical idea. Inside No. 4 Dongtingshan Lane, Guanyao Bridge, South City, in collusion with his sworn brothers Qiu Haining, Zhang Wenzong, Yu Afu, and Shi Asi, he raised funds to fraudulently establish an Xiangshan Shipping Bureau. Wang served as the manager and hired Qiu Aliul and Shi Lichen as partners. They rented a large through-room, inside which were arranged many new-style writing desks, and the four walls were covered with red silk banners celebrating the opening, appearing to be a newly opened shipping bureau. On the one hand, they rented a new Yili steamship from Lifsing to exclusively run the Shanghai and Dinghai line. By this means, they recruited dozens of staff members and tea servants, collected security deposits, and issued bad checks to defraud merchants of goods, totaling approximately 10,000 yuan. Wang and others, taking advantage of the voyage of the rented new Yili steamship to Dinghai on the 27th of this month, absconded with the defrauded goods and money, leaving no trace. Therefore, the defrauded households have not yet been able to take action. There are three cases that have already been discovered. The first case involved the Shengyi Rice Shop at the Great Wharf in South City. On the 26th of this month, a person suddenly came, claiming to be Shi Lichen, the accountant of the Xiangshan Shipping Bureau, who had come to purchase 30 dan of white rice because the bureau needed it. Seeing a large customer coming to the door, the shop provided diligent service and dispatched workers to transport 30 dan of the best white rice (totaling 208 silver dollars) to the bureau. The bureau then issued a check dated the 27th from the Hongxiang Yuji Money Exchange, totaling 208 silver dollars. The next day, the rice shop dispatched worker Qu Gutang to the Hongxiang Bank to cash the check. Unexpectedly, the bank replied that the Xiangshan Shipping Bureau had no funds deposited in the bank. Qu immediately rushed to the bureau to negotiate, but the bureau's manager, Wang Zhihua, had already fled without a trace. At this point, Qu realized that he had been defrauded. He immediately grabbed Shi Lichen, the accountant dispatched by the bureau to purchase the white rice. At the same time, the second case followed closely. On the 26th of this month, the Xianda Rice Shop on Lijie Street at the Great Wharf was also induced by the bureau to dispatch a person to purchase 20 dan of white rice, totaling 138 silver dollars. Afterwards, they also gave the same check that could never be cashed. Upon discovering this, they immediately dispatched worker Wang Changsheng to rush to the bureau to negotiate. He caught sight of the scene and immediately joined forces with Shengyi Rice Shop worker Qu Gusheng to take Shi to the First District General Office. After a preliminary trial by District Chief Guan Gong, he ordered the preparation of an official document and sent them to the bureau for interrogation. Unexpectedly, on the same day (the 27th), shareholder Yu Afu of the bureau went to the Tianqingfu Leather Goods Bureau at Xiaodongmen, falsely claiming that he wanted to purchase several of the best-quality leather furs. Hu Weichu, a partner of the bureau, came out to greet him and took out several of the best-quality leather furs for him to choose from. As a result, they selected five valuable leather furs, such as gray squirrel and gray-backed tan skins, totaling 610 silver dollars. Hu was ordered to send them to the Xiangshan Shipping Bureau, and the bureau issued a check dated the 28th from the Hongxiang Bank, totaling 610 silver dollars. Hu did not suspect anything and returned with the check. Unexpectedly, at approximately 4:00 PM on the 28th (the day before yesterday), when he went to the Hongxiang Bank to cash the check, he was again refused. Realizing that he had been defrauded, he quickly rushed to the bureau, only to find that they had all fled without a trace, and the leather goods were no longer inside the bureau. Only a partner named Qiu Aliul was there guarding the gate. The partner was taken to the First District General Office, and during interrogation by District Chief Guan, Qiu Aliul confessed that Manager Wang Zhihua currently lived in a small room at a certain number in Chongbenli, Guanyao Bridge. The police were immediately dispatched to arrest him, but Wang had already fled upon hearing the news and was not apprehended. His wife, Wang Shi, was taken to the district for questioning. She claimed to know nothing about her husband's actions. It was apparent that the so-called manager of a shipping bureau would not condescend to live in a small room. It was clear that he intended to set up a fraudulent scheme to defraud goods and money. He ordered the preparation of an official document and sent all the people to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation. At the same time, he ordered strict pursuit and arrest of the five major fraudsters, including Wang, so that they could be brought to justice.

A Young Man Attempts Suicide Over Love

Secretly Taking Sleeping Pills to Commit Suicide

Sent to the Hospital for Treatment, Fortunately Resurrected

Li Yuanshan from Ningbo, currently seventeen years old, is an apprentice at a certain domestic goods company in the Penglai Market of this city. He usually has a refined appearance, and being a handsome young man, he has quite a reputation. However, Li is by nature amorous, and his romantic inclinations were awakened early. The foreign entertainment venues by the sea are the easiest place for young people to fall into decline. Thus, Li's footsteps were a daily occurrence in the alleys of pleasure. Furthermore, with his family's wealth, he spent lavishly. Girls love beauty, and pimps love money. Having both, he fell deeper and deeper into decline. There was a Suzhou girl, Xu Jinxian, who was a high-achieving student at a certain girls' school. Now, due to her family's decline, she had no choice but to enter the world of prostitution. She and Li made a vow of love, and he immediately redeemed her and built a love nest in the Shanjiayuan on Baker Road. They were so deeply in love that they seemed to prefer being mandarin ducks to being immortals. Li's family initially did not know about this. Recently, Li's mother, Zhang, believed that her son's immersion in sensual pleasures would ultimately lead to ruin. Therefore, she arranged a marriage for him with the daughter of a certain leather shop owner, Wang, who opened a shop in Sanpailou in the city. The wedding day was set. Initially, Li strongly opposed it, but because he was young, he could not defy his mother's wishes and could only reluctantly agree. When he heard that the wedding day was set, he felt compelled to directly tell his mother his feelings. However, his mother was stubborn and not only refused to allow it but also reprimanded him severely. Li, frustrated by this setback, felt that life was meaningless. One night, he secretly took many sleeping pills in his bedroom. Soon after, the poison took effect, and he began to groan. His mother heard him and immediately sent him by carriage to Renji Hospital in Maijiaquan. Fortunately, he received effective treatment, and his life may be saved. Three suicide notes were found on Li's body, one to his teacher (the manager of the certain domestic goods company), one to his lover Xu Jinxian, and one to his uncle surnamed Huang. The contents were mostly words such as "rather die than be without freedom," and the language was poignant and well-written. A fine young man willing to die for love is pitiable, but his actions are foolish.

Spitting Out Three Taels of Silver

A Worker at the Mint Has a Clever Plan

But Escapes the Eyes of the Inspectors

The Central Mint in Gaochang Temple in the South City has been working day and night to produce silver coins. One night recently (the 28th) at about 1:00 AM, the night shift ended, and the workers left the factory one after another. The inspectors checked the workers as usual. Among them were workers Su Jianting (from Ningbo), 40 years old, and Zhang Rongfu (also from Ningbo), 32 years old. The two had cigarettes in their mouths. The inspectors saw that Su and Zhang looked flustered and immediately searched them. They found nothing. They ordered them to open their mouths and saw that Su Jianting spit out a small piece of silver wrapped in paper, weighing about three taels. Zhang Rongfu spat out a piece of silver from his mouth, weighing about three taels. Both were about an inch square. The men and the loot were immediately detained and reported to the factory director. Yesterday, a formal document was prepared, and the two suspects, Su and Zhang, along with the two small pieces of silver, were transferred to the local court for interrogation.

The Case of Datong Steamship Company Refusing to Register Members

The Labor Union Believes the Actions of Zhengda Steamship Company's Comprador Are Absurd

The Company Issued a Statement Claiming No Obstruction

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that regarding the case of the Datong Steamship Company's Zhengda steamship refusing to register members of the labor union, the Maritime Workers' Union held a committee meeting yesterday to discuss how to respond. The company also issued a statement about the incident. Details are recorded separately below.

Response Measures: The Preparatory Committee of the Chinese Seamen's Union, after receiving a report from the Shanghai branch that the Zhengda steamship's comprador was obstructing the registration of seamen, raised the issue for discussion at the regular meeting yesterday. The proposal stated that the Datong Steamship Company last year, under the pretext of criminal punishment, dismissed four middle-class workers, Jiao Liangcai and others, from the Longda and Zhida steamships. Since the establishment of the union, the workers have repeatedly expressed their suffering and requested reinstatement. After negotiations with the company for several months, there has been no result.

In addition, the order to prevent the registration of seamen, how should it be dealt with? The resolution was: (1) Hand it over to the Guidance Section to send cadres to continue the registration together with the Shanghai branch; (2) Confidential; (3) Send a letter to the Datong Company to inform Zhu Zuoting not to obstruct the labor movement; (4) Regarding the dismissal issue of Jiao Liangcai and others, based on legal points, continue to negotiate with the company; (5) Confidential.

The Labor Union Expresses: Secretary Hou Dachun of the Maritime Workers' Union told the Xinsheng News Agency reporter that the Maritime Workers' Union was organized by the central government and its purpose is to lead and protect the seamen. Carrying out registration is even done by order. Unexpectedly, the Zhengda comprador is actually obstructing it, which is absurd, and even forcing seamen to sign voluntary letters stating that they will not join the union, and confiscating their badges. The union is the leading group of seamen and has the power to correct mistakes. At this time, please continue to persuade in order to resolve the matter as soon as possible, so as not to create further complications. If they are still stubborn, the union has no choice but to submit all the evidence of resistance to the central government for processing.

The Company Defends: The Datong Company issued a statement stating that the company does not prevent or force the cabin boys of the ships from joining the seaman's union, and gives them absolute freedom. Last week, the union sent many people to wait for the ships to arrive, and as soon as the ship arrived, they went aboard and ordered the cabin boys to sign up. On the 21st of this month, the Zhida ship arrived at the port, and the union members again used their old tricks. At this time, it was during the unloading of cargo and passengers, and the cabin boys were very busy with their work. If the union members kept harassing the cabin boys, the order would be disrupted. As a result, they forced one cabin boy, Long Da, to sign up and leave. On the 22nd, the Zhengda ship arrived at the port. In advance, only twenty or more union members went to meet Mr. Zhu, the business director of the ship, claiming to persuade the ship's cabin boys to join the union and asking for assistance. Mr. Zhu replied that whether the cabin boys of the company's ships join the union or not is entirely up to them. If the cabin boys wish to join the union, the company will not prevent them. If they do not wish to join the union, the company is not in a position to force them. The union members replied that it would be good to handle it this way. After Zhengda docked, please ask the cabin boys to introduce them. Mr. Zhu said that the ship had just arrived at the port, and the cabin boys were working and could not be obstructed. After the cargo and passengers were unloaded, I will accompany you on the ship. When Zhengda arrived, a large number of union members went on board immediately. At the same time, Mr. Zhu also boarded the ship. After Mr. Zhu summoned all the cabin boys of the ship, he explained the union's intentions on their behalf. All the cabin boys, after listening, voluntarily expressed that they did not wish to join the union, and then dispersed.

Two Main Criminals in the Assassination of a Secret Agent of the Public Security Bureau Sentenced to Life Imprisonment

Zhang Xinshan, a secret agent of the Detective Team of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, from Anhui Province, nicknamed Xiao Anhui, 29 years old this year, lived in the back building of No. 8 Zhenhua Li, Malang Road, French Concession. He had been in the job for a short time and made enemies with others. On the morning of July 6th of this year, at 8:45 AM, he was stabbed 19 times by enemies with a knife at the entrance of Chongyi Li, No. 459 Malang Road, and died on the spot. The murderer escaped. Detectives from the Police Department found a folding pointed knife at the scene of the crime. Later, the French Police Department's Special Agency and detectives from the Public Security Bureau arrested three suspects, Li Decai, Guo Shanyu, and Guo Yushan, all from the same hometown in Anhui Province, and sent them to the Second Special District Local Court for prosecution. According to the interrogation, Li and others confessed to killing Zhang together. Later, the verdict was that Li Decai and Guo Shanyu were sentenced to life imprisonment for conspiracy to commit murder and deprived of political rights for life. Guo Yushan was sentenced to 20 years in prison and deprived of political rights for 20 years for aiding murder. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that the three criminals, Li and others, were dissatisfied with the original verdict and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court has completed the hearing on the appeal. The day before yesterday afternoon, Judge Guo and Assessors Fan and Sun came to the court and ruled that the original judgment regarding Guo Yushan's crime and sentence was revoked. Guo Yushan was sentenced to 20 years of fixed-term imprisonment for jointly plotting murder. The appeals of Li Decai and Guo Shanyu were rejected. After the judgment, the appellants were still sent back to the detention center to wait for the appeal period of the third instance before being sent to prison for execution.

Dr. Liu Zhanen Prays for Peace

Dr. Liu Zhanen, President of Shanghai University and Councilor of the Shanghai Provisional Municipal Council, has been in the United States for half a year, promoting his country. Dr. Liu has given lectures all over the United States. Recently, due to the recurrence of domestic warfare, he is very concerned. Yesterday, he sent a letter to Mr. Liu Yunfang of the Municipal Council, the original text of which is as follows:

"Yunfang, my brother, I hope you are well. It has been a long time since I last saw you, and I miss you very much. I hope you are well and in good health. I am doing well on my travels and am safe, which is comforting. I am currently giving lectures on Chinese culture throughout the United States at the invitation of American friends. The audience at each lecture is very enthusiastic. I have visited more than 30 cities and met more than 100,000 people. People in that country are very sympathetic to our country and are particularly concerned about Far Eastern affairs. However, I recently read in the newspaper that a civil war is about to break out again in our country. I am deeply saddened by the fratricide. You are highly respected in society and love peace. I hope you will do your best to eliminate it, so as to avoid the increasingly serious national crisis. This is what I, living overseas, pray for day and night. I send this to you with respect and wish you well and a happy new year. Liu Zhanen."

The Central Hotel in Xiaodongmen Has Been Arrested a Large Number of Gamblers Twice

Liu Xuefang, the director of the Second Branch of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently learned that someone was secretly setting up a gambling den in the Central Hotel in Xiaodongmen, gambling heavily. He sent inspectors and police chiefs to investigate secretly, but the gamblers were well-informed and had many hideouts, so they were not caught. At 12:00 AM the night before, Inspector Zhang Panchi suddenly went to inspect and saw a lot of noise in Room 19 on the third floor of the Central Hotel. Knowing something was wrong, he immediately entered the room. The gamblers were having a great time, yelling while gambling. Inspector Zhang immediately arrested them. He arrested seven gamblers, including Gu Mingde, and seized 31 yuan in gambling money, 29 cents in corner tickets, 54 cents in small coins, 159 copper coins, a set of Tianjiu tiles, five copper treasures, and a deck of playing cards. He immediately took them all to the police station for questioning. Director Liu interrogated Gu Mingde, who confessed that he was from Pudong, sold fruit, and lived at No. 18 Dama Tou. Qian Aqing, 34 years old, from Ningbo, lived outside the Guanqiao Bridge. Jiang Songjin, 36 years old, from Ningbo, lived at No. 24 Baodai Lane. Xia Sibao, Chuan A'e, and Zhu Fusheng, from Ningbo. Fang Ruisheng, 32 years old, from Shanghai, all sold fruit and medicinal herbs. While they were being interrogated, it turned out that these gamblers who had escaped the net gathered again after the police arrested them and started gambling again in Room 21 of the Central Hotel. The patrolling police chief Gong Weichuan passed by at 3:00 AM yesterday and arrested 13 more gamblers, including Yao Jingen, and seized a deck of playing cards, 7 yuan in gambling money, 54 cents in small coins, 3 cents in small tickets, and 230 copper coins. They were all taken to the police station for questioning. Director Liu interrogated the defendants Yao Jingen, Ji Chenglin, Chen Guisheng, Zhang A'san, Chen Jinfu, Xie Yongsheng, Xia Azhi, Hu Jingen, Cao Heshang, Cao Fugeng, Liu Jincai, Xu Taotao, and Zhang Caijun, who confessed to gambling but denied taking a cut for profit, saying they were just occasional gatherings. The director believed that during this period of martial law, the gamblers dared to gather in the Central Hotel to gamble heavily and should be presented to the Public Security Bureau for heavy punishment to reassure the people.

Swallowing More Than Twenty Sewing Needles

Ms. Liu Wu Attempts Suicide Due to Economic Pressure

Ms. Liu Wu, from Yangzhou, 40 years old, lives at No. 70 Hexing Li, Yuezhou Road. Due to economic pressure, she suddenly had the idea of ending her life. Fire at Tianfeng Leather Company Injures Three Workers

Yesterday morning at 11:30 AM, a fire broke out at Tianfeng Leather Company, No. 59 Huaxing Fang, Baoding Road, Hongkou, due to excessive heat while boiling oil. The oil in the pot suddenly caught fire. At that time, three workers were working nearby and could not escape in time, resulting in severe burns. People from the company reported to the fire department and sent ambulances to Tongren Hospital for treatment. The names of the injured are as follows: Zhang Guifang, 39 years old; Shi Yongnian, 21 years old; Zhang Haibin, 18 years old. All were injured in the head, face, and hands. It is said that Zhang Guifang was the most seriously injured and may be in danger of dying.

A Girl is Run Over and Killed by a Tram

A Road Worker is Unable to Rescue Her

His Right Hand and Foot Are Also Crushed

The section of East Xihua Road in the middle of Gongping Road and Maohai Road has recently been ordered by the Engineering Department of the Public Works Bureau to send road workers to repair the road. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday at about 4:00 PM, the woman Cao Yin, who lived at No. 38 Longqing Li on that road, had a daughter named Cao Zhaodi, who was only five years old and was playing alone in the middle of the road. At that time, as she was about to cross the road from north to south, a tram No. 77 driven by Sheng Weibin was speeding from the west. He was unable to brake in time and knocked the child down. At the same time, Tang Deming, a road worker from Anhui Province, 23 years old, who was repairing the road there, could not bear to see the child being hit and risked his life to rescue her. But it was too late. The child was crushed and killed. Tang's right hand and foot were also crushed. At the time, West Three Road Toutou No. 303 of the Huishan Patrol Room was also sitting in the car. Suddenly hearing about the accident, he immediately got out of the car, investigated, and reported it to the police station in charge, and ordered an ambulance to send the injured Tang Deming to Tongren Hospital for treatment. After bandaging, he left the hospital. The child's body was sent to the Philan Road Mortuary for an autopsy by detectives who came to investigate. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Diao Chengtang was dispatched to the mortuary by the First Special District Local Court. After examining the body, he took a statement from Tang Deming, who said that he was a road worker and that they were repairing the road at that time. When he saw the child being hit, he wanted to pull her away, but he was also hit and did not know how his hands and feet were injured. Sheng Weibin also said that he was driving the tram and was driving slowly because there were many road workers repairing the road on both sides. The child suddenly ran out from among the workers, so he did not see her. By the time he braked, it was too late. The child's mother, Cao Yin, said that she was washing clothes at home at the time and did not know that the child had gone out. Now that she has been hit and killed, she asked the tram company to provide a coffin and pay for the injured worker's medical expenses. After hearing the statements, Mr. Diao ruled that the deceased girl, Cao Zhaodi, was indeed crushed in the head by the tram No. 77 while she was alive and died. He ordered her mother, Cao Yin, to sign a guarantee to take back the coffin and bury it.

Joint Meeting of the Southern Goods Industry Association

The Southern Goods Industry Association held its 24th executive and supervisory meeting at its premises the day before yesterday. Chairman Gong Jingyan reported on incoming and outgoing documents and then began discussions on: (1) Based on the report from the Evaluation Committee: (A) Member Zaiyang Company has been having a major sale for many days. Staff were sent to advise them, but they refused to accept. This is a deliberate violation of industry regulations. The evidence is conclusive and should be strictly handled. It was resolved to implement Article 7 of Chapter 4 of the industry regulations, revoke their market license, and announce in the newspaper the cancellation of their membership, and report to the higher authorities for record. (B) Yichang Company held a major sale, which led Longchang Company to follow suit, greatly affecting the business of fellow traders. Regarding how to handle this case, it was resolved that the association should request the higher authorities to appoint officials to go with the association's staff to forcibly remove all the lanterns of both parties. The fine will be discussed later. (C) Member Hengsheng Company had hung lanterns, although they have been removed, the prices of goods still do not comply with the association's regulations. Regarding how to handle this case, it was resolved that the company has evidence of price disruption and should be fined 50 yuan in accordance with Article 1 of the industry regulations, as a warning to others. (D) Regarding how to handle cases where non-members of the association violate industry regulations and disrupt prices, it was resolved that the association should send a letter to all the dismantling companies to refuse to trade with them. Accordingly, the above cases were resolved in principle. (2) The association's articles of association were submitted to the higher authorities for approval and record at the time of establishment. Now, the Social Bureau has ordered that several articles should be amended (full text of the proposal), but Article 20 states that the association's income consists of the following items as membership fees: (1) Membership fee of 2 yuan; (2) Monthly membership fee is divided into two types: A 2 yuan, B 1 yuan. According to Committee Member Shen's proposal, the association's finances are indeed insufficient and should be changed to membership fees of four types: A, B, C, and D: 40 yuan for 15 or more people (A), 30 yuan for 10 or more people (B), 20 yuan for 5 or more people (C), and 10 yuan for 2 or more people (D). Monthly membership fees should be based on the number of people using the service, with each person charged 3 jiao per month. Committee Member Xu seconded the motion, and it was resolved to pass it. (3) Discussion: According to the bamboo shoot industry, the price of goods has always been based on the "yue pan" (agreement) as the standard. Recently, due to the Fujian Incident, transportation has been inconvenient, and the "yue pan" needs to be increased by 20%. Regarding what the association should do, it was resolved that the increase in the price of bamboo shoots is a major issue and it was decided to convene a meeting of member representatives on January 5, 23rd year of the Republic, to discuss solutions. The meeting adjourned without discussing other matters.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday said that Shandong Province and the Yellow Sea are cloudy and quite cold, with rain or snow, and the wind direction is uncertain. Here and above the East China Sea, the cyclone is intensifying, with rain or light fog, due to the passage of a low pressure system, moving towards the northeast. There is a wind hurricane southwest of Dongsha Island, which is clearly moving northwest. Its center was within 120 miles of the intersection of 20 degrees north latitude and 115 degrees east longitude at about 6 AM this morning. The wind force is unknown. Also, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 54.3 and the lowest was 43.0. On the same day last year, the highest was 42.4 and the lowest was 34.9.

Letter

To the Editor: In the local news column of your newspaper on the 25th of this month, there was a news item about the Guangxin Dyeing Factory in Lujiabang being bombed, which is somewhat inaccurate. Our factory has always promoted national goods and is determined to expand. It is purely self-woven and self-dyed. Because the original factory site in Lujiabang was insufficient, we built a factory base in Xibaoxing Road, Zhabei, as early as this month, and moved into the new site on the 17th of this month. The machines left at the Lujiabang factory site were taken over by Dahua Dyeing Factory. Therefore, the bombing of the Fuxin Dyeing Factory has nothing to do with our factory. I am writing to request that you publish it in the correction column of your newspaper to avoid confusion. Sincerely, Xin Xin Shengji Dyeing and Weaving Factory Distributor, December 29th.

To the Editor: Your newspaper published a news item on December 13th about the collision between the Wanxiang and Luan Small Ships, and the criticism of me is deeply afraid of causing misunderstandings. I am writing to request a correction and hope you will publish it. The captain of a ship sailing in the outer sea should be fully responsible for driving. However, because the Yangtze River estuary has uncertain currents and depths change from time to time, the ships are driven by Da Er leading the river. Therefore, the collisions and groundings that occur on the way are the responsibility of the leading river on duty. The grounding in Qingpu was actually caused by the leading river mistakenly taking the route. The Wanxiang's collision, the right and wrong are yet to be judged, and the parties involved are the leading river, not the captain. Anyone with a little nautical knowledge knows this. After the incident, all the crew members of this ship engaged in rescue. After the rescue was completed, at 7:50 AM, the anchor was lifted and the ship sailed upstream. At 8:30 PM, it arrived in Han. If the shipowner Leading River hides, the helmsman is beaten, as your newspaper claimed, then who is responsible for lifting the anchor and driving ashore on the way? I hereby write to you, and wish you peace. Sincerely, Weng Jiqing, Captain of the Wanxiang Ship of the Sanbei Company, to the Editor-in-Chief of Shenbao, December 29th.

To the Editor: Today, I found in your newspaper the news that the Da Zhonghua Rubber Factory refused workers to return to work, which was submitted by the Industrial Society. This is not in line with the facts. The party and government authorities have public records of the workers' withdrawal from insurance. In addition to sending staff to directly negotiate with the Industrial Society, our association should ask your newspaper to correct it quickly in order to relieve workers' difficulties and maintain the credibility of the newspaper. Sincerely, Guo Junchen, Director of the Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Second District Rubber Products Industry Union, to the Editor-in-Chief of Shenbao.

Incoming Mail

The Next Year's Plan for Railway Business and Intermodal Transportation (Continued)

(G) Adding Refrigeration Equipment Our country's railways have never had refrigeration transportation equipment, so that fresh goods such as vegetables, fruits, fish, and meat produced on each line cannot be sold smoothly in other places. What is surplus here is exactly what is needed there. The supply and demand is unbalanced, the rural economy is declining day by day, and it is difficult for railway transportation to flourish. Now, in order to solve the problem of regulating the food supply and assisting the rural economy, and at the same time open up a new path for railway business, it seems that it is necessary to quickly carry out refrigeration transportation on the national railways. However, to carry out refrigeration transportation, it is necessary to add equipment such as refrigerated cars and refrigerated warehouses, which requires huge funds and is not easy to raise at once. Now, a plan has been drawn up to be completed in four phases, requiring a total of more than 1.84 million yuan. The funds required in the first year are more than 490,000 yuan, more than 320,000 yuan in the second year, more than 330,000 yuan in the third year, and more than 690,000 yuan in the fourth year. As for the construction steps, the Beijing-Shanghai Railway line has a dense population and a great demand for fresh goods. Moreover, it is closer to the capital and easier to supervise and manage. It is appropriate to give priority to it as a model. Therefore, it is planned to complete it in the first year. The second year has entered the expansion period. In order to make the intermodal transportation of fresh goods developed, the railways connected to it should be continued first. The Tianjin-Pukou Railway is the main north-south line, and the Capital Ferry is now open, so it should be completed in the second year. In the third year, the Shanghai-Hangzhou, Jiaoji, and Longhai Railways, which are close to the Beijing-Shanghai and Tianjin-Pukou Railways, should be continued. The fourth year is the completion period. It is expected that the Guangdong-Guizhou Railway will be completed at that time and will be linked with the Pinghan Railway to form an important north-south line. Therefore, it is planned to complete it in the fourth year.

(H) Holding Exhibitions of Products along the Railway Lines in Beijing, Tianjin, and Qingdao The prosperity or decline of a country's railway business is closely related to the prosperity or decline of the agricultural, industrial, commercial, and mining industries along the line. The prosperity or decline of the agricultural, industrial, commercial, and mining industries along the line depends on the abundance of raw materials and the breadth of sales of manufactured products. Our country has abundant resources, and it is inevitable that there will be more consumption and a wider range of raw materials. However, the places of production are often surplus, and the places of consumption are exhausted. What is discarded here is what is needed there. There is a surplus of domestic products here, and similar foreign goods are used there, causing raw materials to be discarded and industry to decline. The railway's freight volume is reduced due to the sluggishness of various commercial goods, resulting in a daily reduction in income, which is regrettable. In order to awaken the attention of merchants, balance supply and demand, and increase railway business, there is only one way to hold exhibitions of products along the national railway lines, holding them in major commercial ports and large cities in stages by means of a roving exhibition to promote them through publicity. It was held in Shanghai this spring with excellent results. It was held in Beijing this winter with even greater results. It is planned to continue to hold meetings in Beijing, Qingdao, and other places, so that merchants in various places will know the products from all over the country, as well as their quality, price, freight rate, etc., as a reference for business and to promote the progress of industry. Its contribution to the social economy is extraordinary. (To be continued)

Shenbao Radio Weekly

Ultra-Shortwave Radio Telephone

— Jiancun

—Using Electromagnetic Vacuum Tubes Produced by Philips—

Scientific progress often tends towards the peculiar, and radio is no exception. It is now trending towards the review of ultra-shortwaves, and its achievements are becoming more and more remarkable. When Heinrich Hertz conducted experiments on electromagnetic oscillations in 1886-87, the wavelength used was 30 mm, the so-called ultra-shortwave, but people at that time did not know how to use this ultra-shortwave. Therefore, when radio was first put into practical use, the wavelength used was limited to long waves (20,000 to 30,000 meters). Although the use of wavelength gradually tended to be shorter, people at that time thought that only long waves could be used for long-distance communication. Little did they know that the later short waves broke the previous misconception. Not only could they satisfy long-distance communication, but the power they consumed was less than that of long waves.

Since then, short waves have taken the place of long waves. And its application has extended to Televiseon, physics, chemistry and medicine, and its amazing characteristics have gradually become clear. And the ultra-short wavelength we have obtained in the experiment is similar to the wavelength experimented by Hertz that year. According to the experiment conducted by the physical experiment room of the Philips factory, the result of the experiment with a wavelength of one meter is that ultra-short waves can indeed dominate our radio communication industry.

In the experiment, the vacuum tube used to generate the oscillation is the so-called electromagnetic vacuum tube (Magnetrons) with a special structure. The structure of the tube is shown in the figure above. A strong magnetic field is installed in the tube for oscillation. The Philips experiment room has specially designed a suitable structure and circuit diagram for the tube, so that it can be used in parallel connection to obtain extremely high efficiency.

The above picture shows a new type of ultra-shortwave transmitter recently produced by the Philips experiment room. The machine is connected in parallel with two electromagnetic vacuum tubes. It requires 150 watts of input, and a wavelength of about one meter can get 50% efficiency. Compared with the 4% obtained by the System of Barkhausen and Kurz using the same wavelength, the superiority of its efficiency can be seen. If it is only 4% efficiency, it is not difficult to obtain by using the transmitter shown in the figure above and using a wavelength of 55 mm.

Experiments on ultra-shortwaves are still ongoing, but the facts have told us that their application can extend to local broadcasting, secret communication, airway signs, airplanes, and ships for identifying directions in heavy fog.

Ratio of Power to Volume (Continued)—Meaning of Deeibel—

— Li Yuanqing

That is, doubling the power of the radio can probably get three decibels.

Similarly, tripling the power of the radio can probably get five decibels; quadrupling the power can get six decibels; eight times the power can get nine decibels; ten times the power can only get ten decibels, or one bel.... In short, the more the power increases, the less the number of decibels increases.

People with special training in hearing—such as telephone engineers or musicians—can distinguish a change of only one decibel in volume. Ordinary people need a change of three decibels to be able to distinguish the size of the volume.

It is best to avoid mathematical proofs when discussing various scientific problems. Although the formulas borrowed in this article are very simple, I am afraid that they have already aroused the disgust of the general public. Now, in order to make it easier for readers to understand, I will give a simple analogy to explain the above-mentioned special phenomenon.

As shown in the figure, G is a funnel-shaped glass cup, divided into ten grids. First inject one cubic inch of water, assuming it can raise the position of three grids. (That is, reach the height of the third grid) Then inject the same amount of water, because of the large top and small bottom, it will only raise two grids. (The height reaches the fifth grid) Then inject the same amount of water, it can only raise one grid... The higher you go, the less the height increases with the same amount of water added. In the last grid, it takes two cubic inches of water to increase the height by one grid.

Now we compare water to electricity and height to decibels, then it is not difficult to get a clear idea of the relationship between electricity and volume.

This article can be concluded here, but perhaps some people think that the ratio of electricity and volume becoming a logarithm is a scientific misfortune. This is true in theory, but there will be difficulties in fact. Because many noisy sounds in the society (such as gongs and drums, machine sounds, etc.) have great vibration forces. If the feeling of the size of the sound force is a certain proportion, then the brittle eardrum has probably been broken. Therefore, the vibration force and the sound becoming a logarithmic ratio is a very fortunate thing. (End)

The Result of Modulation Exceeding 100%

— Shi Huasheng

Under normal amplitude modulation, the sideband frequency is equal to half the modulation percentage multiplied by the carrier wave amplitude. Therefore, the amplitudes of the lowest and highest tones are actually exactly the same. If we now increase the modulation percentage of the broadcasting machine, then the loudness received by the radio will of course increase proportionally to the rate of increase of the modulation percentage (see the article on the importance of amplitude modulation in the previous issue). The problem now arises here: what will be the result if we increase the modulation percentage to more than one hundred percent? Then the peaks of the sound waves will be cut off. It will sound distorted, and new sidebands will be generated to cause interference. In fact, this simple method can completely disrupt other nearby radio stations on adjacent wavelengths, making it impossible for the listener to discern the music. Therefore, European radio stations, in addition to announcing the wavelength (or frequency) and power, must also report their modulation percentage. This is very important for receiving distant radio stations, because once we understand the principle, we can explain the cause of the problem. Otherwise, interference occurs suddenly, then disappears again, leaving us puzzled and unable to figure it out. In short, a percentage exceeding one hundred is undesirable, except for intentional disruption. A percentage of one hundred or close to one hundred is very beneficial in terms of loudness and can compensate for insufficient power. However, from a musical standpoint, it is better to be less than one hundred percent, such as thirty percent. A compromise of around seventy or eighty percent can take both into consideration.

How to Make a Semi-Variable Shortwave Plug-In Coil

— FR

Features: After the coil is made, its inductance and the closeness of the coupling between the two coils can be increased or decreased at will within a possible range. Because the wires are not wound on other objects, losses can be reduced, so the efficiency is higher than usual. Also, because the diameter of the coil is small, the range reached by the magnetic field lines can be reduced.

Materials: Still use the base of an old vacuum tube, or a specially made plug-in coil tube. For the wires, it is better to use thicker ones for hardness and low resistance: such as number 14 enameled wire is most suitable.

Procedure: Wind the wire in a spiral shape on a round silver-lead pencil, leaving about one or two inches at each end, and then bend it into a right angle according to the method in the attached diagram. Solder the two wire ends to the copper feet of the coil tube. As for the number of turns, it depends on the capacitance of the tuning capacitor.

Adjustment: To increase the inductance of the coil, reduce the distance between the turns. Otherwise, the opposite is true. To make the coupling between the two coils tighter, reduce the distance between the two coils. Otherwise, the opposite is true.

Usage: As usual. However, after the adjustment, the position of the wires should not be changed.

Note: A cylinder with the same diameter as the inner diameter of the coil tube can be placed on this coil to avoid changing the position of the wires. If a copper or aluminum cylinder is used, it can not only prevent bumping, but also serve as a shield.

Color Codes for Standard Wiring

— Yizhi

Wireless equipment circuits are becoming increasingly complex. Taking a look inside, the wiring is chaotic and crisscrossed. If a problem occurs, it is really difficult for the repairer to start. Therefore, the American International Electrical Manufacturers Association has set a standard wiring system to facilitate inspection and repair. Many American radios sold on the market now use the standard wiring system set by the association.

Standard wiring uses the color of the wire to distinguish which part it is connected to. B+ (amplification) is designated as red, B+ (detection) as brown, B- as black with a slight red tint, C+ as cyan, C- (low) as black and cyan, C- (high) as black with a slight cyan tint, speaker (connected to the plate end) as black with a slight brown tint, speaker (connected to the screen grid end) as brown, speaker excitation coil, one as red, A+ as black, and A- as black with a slight yellow tint.

Education News - Other Cities

Ministry of Education Explains Regulations for Middle School Student Entrance Examinations

The Ministry of Education, based on requests from the Jiangsu Education Department and the Nanjing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau for clarification of ambiguous points in the regulations for middle school student graduation entrance examinations, has issued separate explanations and directives to the relevant departments to comply with. The explanation directives are excerpted below:

Ministry of Education Directive to the Jiangsu Education Department Regarding Requests for Interpretation of Ambiguities in the Regulations for Middle School Student Graduation Entrance Examinations and the Regulations for the Entrance Examination Committee: Your submission has been reviewed. The questions raised in your submission are explained point by point below: (1) If middle schools under the jurisdiction of education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities have classes that start in the spring, then graduation entrance examinations must be held twice a year. Students who repeat a grade can participate in the next entrance examination. Therefore, repeating a grade twice is, in effect, equivalent to repeating a grade for only one academic year. If parents are unable to bear the burden or students are unwilling to repeat the grade again, the original school may issue a certificate of completion of studies. (2) Senior middle schools are allowed to enroll students with equivalent academic qualifications, which has already been clearly stipulated by the Ministry in the middle school regulations and does not need to be restated in the entrance examination regulations. Junior middle school students who fail one or two subjects may take the entrance examination for higher education with equivalent academic qualifications. (3) The graduation entrance examination pass certificate is not a graduation certificate. This certificate is prepared by the department and issued within two weeks after the entrance examination for students to use for admission to higher education and examinations. The graduation certificate should be annotated with the words "passed the entrance examination," stamped by the department, and then issued by the original school. (4) The provision that members of the examination setting committee and the invigilation committee may not be filled by faculty members of schools participating in the entrance examination should still be complied with.

Germany to Limit the Number of University Students Nationwide Starting Next Year

Preventing Overcrowding in Schools

Total Number Set at 15,000

(Berlin, 28th, Reuters) According to the regulations announced by the government today, in order to prevent overcrowding in schools, only a portion of young people will be able to enjoy education in German universities in the future. Starting next year, the total number of university students in Germany will be limited to 15,000, with a ratio of ten men to one woman. The selection of all applicants will be based on their physical fitness, morality, and superior national character. Since 1926, the average annual number of people entering university has been 28,000, but this will decrease in the future.

Architect Wu Baihua Returns to China

Architect Wu Baihua graduated from Tsinghua University in 1928 and went to Europe to specialize in architecture and municipal administration. In 1933, he graduated from the Paris School of Architecture. His graduation design, "Europe's Highest Institution of Learning," was grand in scale and magnificent in design. He won the school's first gold medal. After graduation, he was hired as an assistant by Mr. Lu Bolut, chief architect of the French government. He designed the French Embassy in Turkey and the headquarters of the Paris Electric Company. This summer, in October, the International Architectural Conference was held in Italy. Mr. Wu was invited to the conference, where he exchanged ideas with famous architects from all over the world among the famous mountains and rivers of Italy. He gained particular insights into the new architectural styles of various countries. His return to China this time will bring new contributions to the architecture of our country.

Puppet State Participation in Far Eastern Games, China Decides to Withdraw

Philippines Invites Discussion on Puppet State Participation

Association Replies by Telegram, Refuses to Send Representatives

Manchuria, lost territory, has surprisingly formed its own sports association and sent a letter this spring requesting to join the Far Eastern Games as a member, hoping to attend the tenth competition. The matter is suspicious, and the background clearly involves a conspiracy by certain foreigners to embarrass China. The request was sent to the Philippine Athletic Association, which inquired about China's opinion. The National Sports Association of China, upon receiving the news, resolutely rejected the application on the grounds that Manchuria is not a formal nation and stated that if Japan and the Philippines disregarded its position in the League of Nations and accommodated the application, China would have no choice but to withdraw from the Far Eastern Games and would not compromise. It is now learned that last week, the National Sports Association received a telegram from the Philippine Athletic Association stating, "Regarding the requests from Vietnam, Manchuria, and the Dutch East Indies to join as members, a meeting of representatives from the three countries will be convened in the Philippines at the end of January next year to discuss solutions. Please send a representative from China to attend," and so on. The association convened a board meeting on the 26th to discuss countermeasures and decided to reply to the Philippine Athletic Association, the gist of which is as follows: "Regarding the so-called Manchurian state still being included in the new membership matter, we regret that we cannot send a representative to attend the meeting." —Result: 30-29—

Hujiang University's basketball team lost to Jiaotong University by one point yesterday, with a score of 29-30. After the start of the game, Hujiang took the initiative, launching a fierce attack. Wang Dian and Shi Hengzhi scored three consecutive times, taking a commanding lead of 6-0. On the other hand, Jiaotong University's momentum was strong, and their energy was extraordinary, scoring repeatedly, and the score increased sharply to 15-9. Hujiang was pushed into a disadvantage, so they worked hard to make progress.
